from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass, field

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import torch.nn.functional as F
import triton
import triton.language as tl

EPS = 1.0e-6
GROUP_SIZE = 128


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class Config:
    hidden: int = 2304
    kda_heads: int = 32
    kda_head_dim: int = 128
    short_conv: int = 4
    mla_heads: int = 32
    kv_lora: int = 512
    qk_nope: int = 128
    qk_rope: int = 64
    v_head: int = 128
    rope_theta: float = 10000.0
    n_experts: int = 64
    n_active: int = 8
    n_shared: int = 1
    moe_inter: int = 1024
    routed_scaling: float = 2.446
    group: int = 128
    pattern: tuple = ("K", "K", "K", "M")
    dtype: torch.dtype = field(default=torch.bfloat16)


def build_config(shape: dict) -> Config:
    return Config(n_experts=int(shape.get("n_experts", 64)))


def _rmsnorm(x: torch.Tensor, w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    xf = x.float()
    xf = xf * torch.rsqrt(xf.pow(2).mean(-1, keepdim=True) + EPS)
    return (xf * w.float()).to(x.dtype)


def _rope_cossin(pos: int, dim: int, theta: float, device):
    inv = 1.0 / (theta ** (torch.arange(0, dim, 2, device=device, dtype=torch.float32) / dim))
    ang = pos * inv
    return torch.cos(ang), torch.sin(ang)


def _apply_rope(x: torch.Tensor, cos: torch.Tensor, sin: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    xf = x.float()
    even, odd = xf[..., 0::2], xf[..., 1::2]
    out = torch.empty_like(xf)
    out[..., 0::2] = even * cos - odd * sin
    out[..., 1::2] = odd * cos + even * sin
    return out.to(x.dtype)


@triton.jit
def _rmsnorm_kernel(x, w, y, N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
    offs = tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
    mask = offs < N
    xv = tl.load(x + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    ss = tl.sum(xv * xv, axis=0) / N
    r = tl.rsqrt(ss + 1.0e-6)
    wv = tl.load(w + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    tl.store(y + offs, xv * r * wv, mask=mask)


@triton.jit
def _router_kernel(x, weight, idx_out, w_out, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr,
                   SCALE: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
    offs_n = tl.arange(0, 64)
    offs_k = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
    acc = tl.zeros((64,), tl.float32)
    for k0 in range(0, K, BLOCK_K):
        kk = k0 + offs_k
        xv = tl.load(x + kk).to(tl.float32)[None, :]
        wv = tl.load(weight + offs_n[:, None] * K + kk[None, :]).to(tl.float32)
        acc += tl.sum(wv * xv, axis=1)

    vals = acc
    m0, i0 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i0, -float("inf"), vals)
    m1, i1 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i1, -float("inf"), vals)
    m2, i2 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i2, -float("inf"), vals)
    m3, i3 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i3, -float("inf"), vals)
    m4, i4 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i4, -float("inf"), vals)
    m5, i5 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i5, -float("inf"), vals)
    m6, i6 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i6, -float("inf"), vals)
    m7, i7 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)

    e0 = 1.0
    e1 = tl.exp(m1 - m0)
    e2 = tl.exp(m2 - m0)
    e3 = tl.exp(m3 - m0)
    e4 = tl.exp(m4 - m0)
    e5 = tl.exp(m5 - m0)
    e6 = tl.exp(m6 - m0)
    e7 = tl.exp(m7 - m0)
    den = e0 + e1 + e2 + e3 + e4 + e5 + e6 + e7 + 1.0e-9
    s = SCALE / den
    tl.store(idx_out + 0, i0)
    tl.store(idx_out + 1, i1)
    tl.store(idx_out + 2, i2)
    tl.store(idx_out + 3, i3)
    tl.store(idx_out + 4, i4)
    tl.store(idx_out + 5, i5)
    tl.store(idx_out + 6, i6)
    tl.store(idx_out + 7, i7)
    tl.store(w_out + 0, e0 * s)
    tl.store(w_out + 1, e1 * s)
    tl.store(w_out + 2, e2 * s)
    tl.store(w_out + 3, e3 * s)
    tl.store(w_out + 4, e4 * s)
    tl.store(w_out + 5, e5 * s)
    tl.store(w_out + 6, e6 * s)
    tl.store(w_out + 7, e7 * s)


@triton.jit
def _beta_kernel(x, weight, y, K: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
    offs_n = tl.arange(0, 32)
    offs_k = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
    acc = tl.zeros((32,), tl.float32)
    for k0 in range(0, K, BLOCK_K):
        kk = k0 + offs_k
        xv = tl.load(x + kk).to(tl.float32)[None, :]
        wv = tl.load(weight + offs_n[:, None] * K + kk[None, :]).to(tl.float32)
        acc += tl.sum(wv * xv, axis=1)
    tl.store(y + offs_n, tl.sigmoid(acc))


@triton.jit
def _gemv_kernel(x, wq, scales, zeros, y, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr,
                 BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
        p = p0 + offs_p
        byte = tl.load(wq + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
        group = p // 64
        s = tl.load(scales + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(zeros + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        x0 = tl.load(x + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
        x1 = tl.load(x + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
        lo = (byte & 15).to(tl.float32)
        hi = ((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
        acc += tl.sum(((lo - z) * x0 + (hi - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=offs_n < N)


@triton.jit
def _gemv4_kernel(x, wq0, sc0, ze0, y0, wq1, sc1, ze1, y1, wq2, sc2, ze2, y2,
                  wq3, sc3, ze3, y3, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr,
                  BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
    acc0 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    acc1 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    acc2 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    acc3 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
        p = p0 + offs_p
        group = p // 64
        x0 = tl.load(x + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
        x1 = tl.load(x + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]

        byte = tl.load(wq0 + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
        s = tl.load(sc0 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(ze0 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc0 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)

        byte = tl.load(wq1 + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
        s = tl.load(sc1 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(ze1 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc1 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)

        byte = tl.load(wq2 + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
        s = tl.load(sc2 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(ze2 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc2 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)

        byte = tl.load(wq3 + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
        s = tl.load(sc3 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(ze3 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc3 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)

    tl.store(y0 + offs_n, acc0, mask=offs_n < N)
    tl.store(y1 + offs_n, acc1, mask=offs_n < N)
    tl.store(y2 + offs_n, acc2, mask=offs_n < N)
    tl.store(y3 + offs_n, acc3, mask=offs_n < N)


@triton.jit
def _expert_gemv2_kernel(x, idx, wq0, sc0, ze0, y0, wq1, sc1, ze1, y1,
                         K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
                         BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    e = tl.load(idx + pid_e)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
    acc0 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    acc1 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    w_base = e * ((K // 2) * N)
    q_base = e * (NG * N)
    for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
        p = p0 + offs_p
        group = p // 64
        x0 = tl.load(x + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
        x1 = tl.load(x + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]

        byte = tl.load(wq0 + w_base + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
        s = tl.load(sc0 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(ze0 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc0 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)

        byte = tl.load(wq1 + w_base + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
        s = tl.load(sc1 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(ze1 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc1 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
    out = pid_e * N + offs_n
    tl.store(y0 + out, acc0, mask=offs_n < N)
    tl.store(y1 + out, acc1, mask=offs_n < N)


@triton.jit
def _short_conv3_kernel(q, k, v, cq, ck, cv, conv_w, C: tl.constexpr, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
    offs = tl.program_id(0) * BLOCK + tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
    mask = offs < C

    qv = tl.load(q + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    p0 = tl.load(cq + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    p1 = tl.load(cq + C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    p2 = tl.load(cq + 2 * C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w0 = tl.load(conv_w + offs * 4, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w1 = tl.load(conv_w + offs * 4 + 1, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w2 = tl.load(conv_w + offs * 4 + 2, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w3 = tl.load(conv_w + offs * 4 + 3, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    out = p0 * w0 + p1 * w1 + p2 * w2 + qv * w3
    tl.store(q + offs, out * tl.sigmoid(out), mask=mask)
    tl.store(cq + offs, p1, mask=mask)
    tl.store(cq + C + offs, p2, mask=mask)
    tl.store(cq + 2 * C + offs, qv, mask=mask)

    kv = tl.load(k + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    p0 = tl.load(ck + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    p1 = tl.load(ck + C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    p2 = tl.load(ck + 2 * C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    base = C * 4
    w0 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w1 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4 + 1, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w2 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4 + 2, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w3 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4 + 3, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    out = p0 * w0 + p1 * w1 + p2 * w2 + kv * w3
    tl.store(k + offs, out * tl.sigmoid(out), mask=mask)
    tl.store(ck + offs, p1, mask=mask)
    tl.store(ck + C + offs, p2, mask=mask)
    tl.store(ck + 2 * C + offs, kv, mask=mask)

    vv = tl.load(v + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    p0 = tl.load(cv + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    p1 = tl.load(cv + C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    p2 = tl.load(cv + 2 * C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    base = 2 * C * 4
    w0 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w1 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4 + 1, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w2 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4 + 2, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    w3 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4 + 3, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    out = p0 * w0 + p1 * w1 + p2 * w2 + vv * w3
    tl.store(v + offs, out * tl.sigmoid(out), mask=mask)
    tl.store(cv + offs, p1, mask=mask)
    tl.store(cv + C + offs, p2, mask=mask)
    tl.store(cv + 2 * C + offs, vv, mask=mask)


@triton.jit
def _kda_recur_kernel(q, k, v, gp, beta, S, o, D: tl.constexpr,
                      SCALE: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_V: tl.constexpr):
    h = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_v = tl.program_id(1)
    offs_d = tl.arange(0, 128)
    offs_v = pid_v * BLOCK_V + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_V)
    base = h * D
    s_base = h * D * D
    s_offs = s_base + offs_d[:, None] * D + offs_v[None, :]

    qv = tl.load(q + base + offs_d).to(tl.float32) * SCALE
    kv = tl.load(k + base + offs_d).to(tl.float32)
    gv = tl.load(gp + base + offs_d).to(tl.float32)
    decay = tl.sigmoid(-gv)
    vv = tl.load(v + base + offs_v, mask=offs_v < D, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    b = tl.load(beta + h).to(tl.float32)

    sold = tl.load(S + s_offs, mask=offs_v[None, :] < D, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    sdec = sold * decay[:, None]
    pred = tl.sum(sdec * kv[:, None], axis=0)
    snew = sdec + (b * kv)[:, None] * (vv[None, :] - pred[None, :])
    out = tl.sum(snew * qv[:, None], axis=0)

    tl.store(S + s_offs, snew, mask=offs_v[None, :] < D)
    tl.store(o + base + offs_v, out, mask=offs_v < D)


@triton.jit
def _expert_hidden_kernel(x, idx, wq0, sc0, ze0, wq1, sc1, ze1, y,
                          K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
                          BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    e = tl.load(idx + pid_e)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
    acc0 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    acc1 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    w_base = e * ((K // 2) * N)
    q_base = e * (NG * N)
    for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
        p = p0 + offs_p
        group = p // 64
        x0 = tl.load(x + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
        x1 = tl.load(x + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]

        byte = tl.load(wq0 + w_base + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
        s = tl.load(sc0 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(ze0 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc0 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)

        byte = tl.load(wq1 + w_base + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
        s = tl.load(sc1 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(ze1 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc1 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
    h = (acc0 * tl.sigmoid(acc0)) * acc1
    tl.store(y + pid_e * N + offs_n, h, mask=offs_n < N)


@triton.jit
def _expert_hidden_mix_kernel(x, idx, wq0, sc0, ze0, wq1, sc1, ze1,
                              swq0, ssc0, sze0, swq1, ssc1, sze1, y,
                              K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
                              R: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
                              BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    is_shared = pid_e == R
    e = tl.load(idx + pid_e, mask=pid_e < R, other=0)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
    acc0 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    acc1 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    w_base = e * ((K // 2) * N)
    q_base = e * (NG * N)
    for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
        p = p0 + offs_p
        group = p // 64
        x0 = tl.load(x + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
        x1 = tl.load(x + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]

        ptr = tl.where(is_shared, swq0 + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
                       wq0 + w_base + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :])
        sptr = tl.where(is_shared, ssc0 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
                        sc0 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :])
        zptr = tl.where(is_shared, sze0 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
                        ze0 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :])
        byte = tl.load(ptr, mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
        s = tl.load(sptr, mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(zptr, mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc0 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)

        ptr = tl.where(is_shared, swq1 + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
                       wq1 + w_base + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :])
        sptr = tl.where(is_shared, ssc1 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
                        sc1 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :])
        zptr = tl.where(is_shared, sze1 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :],
                        ze1 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :])
        byte = tl.load(ptr, mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
        s = tl.load(sptr, mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(zptr, mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc1 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
    h = (acc0 * tl.sigmoid(acc0)) * acc1
    tl.store(y + pid_e * N + offs_n, h, mask=offs_n < N)


@triton.jit
def _expert_down_sum_kernel(x, route_w, idx, wq, scales, zeros, y,
                            K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
                            ESEL: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
                            BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr, ADD: tl.constexpr):
    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    for jj in range(0, ESEL):
        e = tl.load(idx + jj)
        rw = tl.load(route_w + jj).to(tl.float32)
        w_base = e * ((K // 2) * N)
        q_base = e * (NG * N)
        eacc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
        for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
            p = p0 + offs_p
            group = p // 64
            x0 = tl.load(x + jj * K + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
            x1 = tl.load(x + jj * K + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
            byte = tl.load(wq + w_base + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
            s = tl.load(scales + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
            z = tl.load(zeros + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
            eacc += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
        acc += rw * eacc
    if ADD:
        acc += tl.load(y + offs_n, mask=offs_n < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=offs_n < N)


@triton.jit
def _expert_down_mix_kernel(x, route_w, idx, wq, scales, zeros, swq, sscales, szeros, y,
                            K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
                            R: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr,
                            BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    for jj in range(0, R + 1):
        eacc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
        if jj < R:
            e = tl.load(idx + jj)
            rw = tl.load(route_w + jj).to(tl.float32)
            w_base = e * ((K // 2) * N)
            q_base = e * (NG * N)
            for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
                p = p0 + offs_p
                group = p // 64
                x0 = tl.load(x + jj * K + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
                x1 = tl.load(x + jj * K + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
                byte = tl.load(wq + w_base + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
                s = tl.load(scales + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
                z = tl.load(zeros + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
                eacc += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
            acc += rw * eacc
        else:
            for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
                p = p0 + offs_p
                group = p // 64
                x0 = tl.load(x + jj * K + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
                x1 = tl.load(x + jj * K + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
                byte = tl.load(swq + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
                s = tl.load(sscales + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
                z = tl.load(szeros + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
                eacc += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
            acc += eacc
    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=offs_n < N)


@triton.jit
def _mla_alpha_kernel(q, wq, scales, zeros, alpha,
                      H: tl.constexpr, K: tl.constexpr, STRIDE_Q: tl.constexpr,
                      STRIDE_HEAD: tl.constexpr, N_TOTAL: tl.constexpr,
                      BLOCK_R: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_D: tl.constexpr):
    pid_h = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_r = tl.program_id(1)
    offs_r = pid_r * BLOCK_R + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_R)
    offs_d = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_D)
    cols = pid_h * STRIDE_HEAD + offs_d
    byte = tl.load(wq + (offs_r[:, None] // 2) * N_TOTAL + cols[None, :],
                   mask=offs_r[:, None] < K, other=0)
    s = tl.load(scales + (offs_r[:, None] // 128) * N_TOTAL + cols[None, :],
                mask=offs_r[:, None] < K, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    z = tl.load(zeros + (offs_r[:, None] // 128) * N_TOTAL + cols[None, :],
                mask=offs_r[:, None] < K, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
    lo = (byte & 15).to(tl.float32)
    hi = ((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
    use_hi = (offs_r[:, None] & 1) == 1
    w = tl.where(use_hi, hi, lo)
    qv = tl.load(q + pid_h * STRIDE_Q + offs_d).to(tl.float32)[None, :]
    acc = tl.sum((w - z) * s * qv, axis=1)
    tl.store(alpha + pid_h * K + offs_r, acc, mask=offs_r < K)


@triton.jit
def _mla_value_kernel(latent, wq, scales, zeros, out,
                      K: tl.constexpr, N_HEAD: tl.constexpr, STRIDE_HEAD: tl.constexpr,
                      N_TOTAL: tl.constexpr, VALUE_OFF: tl.constexpr,
                      BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
    pid_h = tl.program_id(0)
    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
    offs_nh = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
    cols = pid_h * STRIDE_HEAD + VALUE_OFF + offs_nh
    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
    for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
        p = p0 + offs_p
        group = p // 64
        x0 = tl.load(latent + pid_h * K + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
        x1 = tl.load(latent + pid_h * K + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
        byte = tl.load(wq + p[:, None] * N_TOTAL + cols[None, :], mask=offs_nh[None, :] < N_HEAD, other=0)
        s = tl.load(scales + group[:, None] * N_TOTAL + cols[None, :], mask=offs_nh[None, :] < N_HEAD, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        z = tl.load(zeros + group[:, None] * N_TOTAL + cols[None, :], mask=offs_nh[None, :] < N_HEAD, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
        acc += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
    tl.store(out + pid_h * N_HEAD + offs_nh, acc, mask=offs_nh < N_HEAD)


def _lin(x: torch.Tensor, ql: "QuantLinear") -> torch.Tensor:
    y = torch.empty((ql.out_f,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    if ql.in_f == 4096:
        block_n, block_p, warps = 8, 512, 8
    elif ql.out_f <= 1024:
        block_n, block_p, warps = 8, 128, 8
    else:
        block_n, block_p, warps = 32, 128, 4
    _gemv_kernel[(triton.cdiv(ql.out_f, block_n),)](
        x, ql.w_q, ql.scales, ql.zeros, y, ql.in_f, ql.out_f,
        BLOCK_N=block_n, BLOCK_P=block_p,
        num_warps=warps,
    )
    return y


def _lin4(x: torch.Tensor, a: "QuantLinear", b: "QuantLinear", c: "QuantLinear",
          d: "QuantLinear"):
    y0 = torch.empty((a.out_f,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    y1 = torch.empty_like(y0)
    y2 = torch.empty_like(y0)
    y3 = torch.empty_like(y0)
    _gemv4_kernel[(triton.cdiv(a.out_f, 16),)](
        x, a.w_q, a.scales, a.zeros, y0, b.w_q, b.scales, b.zeros, y1,
        c.w_q, c.scales, c.zeros, y2, d.w_q, d.scales, d.zeros, y3,
        a.in_f, a.out_f, BLOCK_N=16, BLOCK_P=128, num_warps=8,
    )
    return y0, y1, y2, y3


def _fast_rmsnorm(x: torch.Tensor, w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
    y = torch.empty_like(x)
    _rmsnorm_kernel[(1,)](x, w, y, x.numel(), BLOCK=4096, num_warps=8)
    return y


def _route(x: torch.Tensor, router: nn.Linear, scaling: float):
    idx = torch.empty((8,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.long)
    w = torch.empty((8,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
    _router_kernel[(1,)](x, router.weight, idx, w, x.numel(), router.out_features, scaling,
                         BLOCK_K=256, num_warps=8)
    return w, idx


def _beta(x: torch.Tensor, proj: nn.Linear) -> torch.Tensor:
    y = torch.empty((32,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
    _beta_kernel[(1,)](x, proj.weight, y, x.numel(), BLOCK_K=256, num_warps=8)
    return y


class QuantLinear(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, in_f: int, out_f: int, group: int = GROUP_SIZE):
        super().__init__()
        self.in_f, self.out_f, self.group = in_f, out_f, group
        ng = in_f // group
        self.register_buffer("w_q", torch.zeros(in_f // 2, out_f, dtype=torch.uint8))
        self.register_buffer("scales", torch.zeros(ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
        self.register_buffer("zeros", torch.zeros(ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))

    def forward(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
        return _lin(x, self)


class QuantExperts(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, n: int, in_f: int, out_f: int, group: int = GROUP_SIZE):
        super().__init__()
        self.n, self.in_f, self.out_f, self.group = n, in_f, out_f, group
        ng = in_f // group
        self.register_buffer("w_q", torch.zeros(n, in_f // 2, out_f, dtype=torch.uint8))
        self.register_buffer("scales", torch.zeros(n, ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))
        self.register_buffer("zeros", torch.zeros(n, ng, out_f, dtype=torch.bfloat16))


class KDA(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        H, Dk, d = cfg.kda_heads, cfg.kda_head_dim, cfg.hidden
        self.q_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.k_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.v_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.g_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * Dk, cfg.group)
        self.beta_proj = nn.Linear(d, H, bias=False, dtype=cfg.dtype)
        self.conv_w = nn.Parameter(torch.empty(3, H * Dk, cfg.short_conv, dtype=cfg.dtype))
        self.o_proj = QuantLinear(H * Dk, d, cfg.group)
        self.scale = Dk ** -0.5

    def _short_conv(self, val, prev, idx):
        win = torch.cat([prev, val[None]], dim=0)
        w = self.conv_w[idx].float().transpose(0, 1)
        out = (win.float() * w).sum(0)
        return F.silu(out).to(val.dtype), win[1:]

    def step(self, x, st):
        H, Dk = self.cfg.kda_heads, self.cfg.kda_head_dim
        q, k, v, gp = _lin4(x, self.q_proj, self.k_proj, self.v_proj, self.g_proj)
        _short_conv3_kernel[(triton.cdiv(H * Dk, 256),)](
            q, k, v, st["cq"], st["ck"], st["cv"], self.conv_w, H * Dk,
            BLOCK=256, num_warps=4,
        )
        beta = _beta(x, self.beta_proj)
        o = torch.empty((H * Dk,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        _kda_recur_kernel[(H, triton.cdiv(Dk, 16))](
            q, k, v, gp, beta, st["S"], o, Dk, self.scale, BLOCK_V=16, num_warps=4,
        )
        return _lin(o, self.o_proj)


class MLA(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        H, d = cfg.mla_heads, cfg.hidden
        self.q_proj = QuantLinear(d, H * (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope), cfg.group)
        self.kv_a = QuantLinear(d, cfg.kv_lora + cfg.qk_rope, cfg.group)
        self.kv_b = QuantLinear(cfg.kv_lora, H * (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.v_head), cfg.group)
        self.o_proj = QuantLinear(H * cfg.v_head, d, cfg.group)
        self.scale = (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope) ** -0.5

    def _append_cache(self, st, c_new, k_new, pos):
        cfg = self.cfg
        buf = st.get("_c_buf")
        rbuf = st.get("_r_buf")
        if buf is None or pos >= buf.shape[0]:
            cap = max(pos + 64, max(pos + 1, int((pos + 1) * 1.25)))
            buf = torch.empty((cap, cfg.kv_lora), device=c_new.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
            rbuf = torch.empty((cap, cfg.qk_rope), device=c_new.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
            if pos:
                buf[:pos].copy_(st["c_kv"])
                rbuf[:pos].copy_(st["k_rope"])
            st["_c_buf"] = buf
            st["_r_buf"] = rbuf
        buf[pos].copy_(c_new)
        rbuf[pos].copy_(k_new)
        st["c_kv"] = buf[: pos + 1]
        st["k_rope"] = rbuf[: pos + 1]

    def step(self, x, st):
        cfg = self.cfg
        H = cfg.mla_heads
        pos = int(st.get("_pos", st["c_kv"].shape[0]))
        q = _lin(x, self.q_proj).view(H, cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope)
        q_nope = q[:, : cfg.qk_nope]
        q_rope = q[:, cfg.qk_nope :]
        kv = _lin(x, self.kv_a)
        c_new = kv[: cfg.kv_lora]
        k_new = kv[cfg.kv_lora :]
        cos, sin = _rope_cossin(pos, cfg.qk_rope, cfg.rope_theta, x.device)
        q_rope = _apply_rope(q_rope, cos, sin)
        k_new = _apply_rope(k_new, cos, sin)
        self._append_cache(st, c_new, k_new, pos)
        st["_pos"] = pos + 1

        alpha = torch.empty((H, cfg.kv_lora), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        _mla_alpha_kernel[(H, triton.cdiv(cfg.kv_lora, 16))](
            q_nope, self.kv_b.w_q, self.kv_b.scales, self.kv_b.zeros, alpha,
            H, cfg.kv_lora, cfg.qk_nope + cfg.qk_rope, cfg.qk_nope + cfg.v_head,
            H * (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.v_head), BLOCK_R=16, BLOCK_D=128,
            num_warps=4,
        )
        scores = alpha @ st["c_kv"].t()
        scores = scores.float()
        scores += q_rope.float() @ st["k_rope"].float().t()
        scores *= self.scale
        p = torch.softmax(scores, dim=-1)
        latent = (p.to(torch.bfloat16) @ st["c_kv"]).to(torch.bfloat16)
        o = torch.empty((H, cfg.v_head), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        _mla_value_kernel[(H, triton.cdiv(cfg.v_head, 32))](
            latent, self.kv_b.w_q, self.kv_b.scales, self.kv_b.zeros, o,
            cfg.kv_lora, cfg.v_head, cfg.qk_nope + cfg.v_head,
            H * (cfg.qk_nope + cfg.v_head), cfg.qk_nope,
            BLOCK_N=32, BLOCK_P=64, num_warps=4,
        )
        return _lin(o.reshape(H * cfg.v_head), self.o_proj)


class MoE(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        d, m, E = cfg.hidden, cfg.moe_inter, cfg.n_experts
        self.router = nn.Linear(d, E, bias=False, dtype=cfg.dtype)
        self.gate = QuantExperts(E, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.up = QuantExperts(E, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.down = QuantExperts(E, m, d, cfg.group)
        self.s_gate = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.s_up = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.s_down = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, m, d, cfg.group)
        self.register_buffer("_shared_idx", torch.zeros(cfg.n_shared, dtype=torch.long), persistent=False)
        self.register_buffer("_shared_w", torch.ones(cfg.n_shared, dtype=torch.bfloat16), persistent=False)

    def _hidden(self, x, idx, gate, up):
        cfg = self.cfg
        y = torch.empty((idx.numel(), cfg.moe_inter), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        _expert_hidden_kernel[(idx.numel(), triton.cdiv(cfg.moe_inter, 32))](
            x, idx, gate.w_q, gate.scales, gate.zeros, up.w_q, up.scales, up.zeros, y,
            gate.in_f, gate.out_f, gate.in_f // gate.group, BLOCK_N=32, BLOCK_P=128,
            num_warps=4,
        )
        return y

    def _down_sum(self, h, rw, idx, down, out=None, add=False):
        cfg = self.cfg
        if out is None:
            out = torch.empty((cfg.hidden,), device=h.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        _expert_down_sum_kernel[(triton.cdiv(cfg.hidden, 8),)](
            h, rw, idx, down.w_q, down.scales, down.zeros, out,
            down.in_f, down.out_f, down.in_f // down.group, idx.numel(),
            BLOCK_N=8, BLOCK_P=256, ADD=add, num_warps=4,
        )
        return out

    def step(self, x):
        cfg = self.cfg
        w, idx = _route(x, self.router, cfg.routed_scaling)
        h = torch.empty((cfg.n_active + cfg.n_shared, cfg.moe_inter), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        _expert_hidden_mix_kernel[(cfg.n_active + cfg.n_shared, triton.cdiv(cfg.moe_inter, 32))](
            x, idx, self.gate.w_q, self.gate.scales, self.gate.zeros,
            self.up.w_q, self.up.scales, self.up.zeros,
            self.s_gate.w_q, self.s_gate.scales, self.s_gate.zeros,
            self.s_up.w_q, self.s_up.scales, self.s_up.zeros, h,
            self.gate.in_f, self.gate.out_f, self.gate.in_f // self.gate.group,
            cfg.n_active, BLOCK_N=32, BLOCK_P=128, num_warps=4,
        )
        out = torch.empty((cfg.hidden,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
        _expert_down_mix_kernel[(triton.cdiv(cfg.hidden, 8),)](
            h, w, idx, self.down.w_q, self.down.scales, self.down.zeros,
            self.s_down.w_q, self.s_down.scales, self.s_down.zeros, out,
            self.down.in_f, self.down.out_f, self.down.in_f // self.down.group,
            cfg.n_active, BLOCK_N=8, BLOCK_P=512, num_warps=4,
        )
        return out


class Block(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg, kind):
        super().__init__()
        self.kind = kind
        self.attn_norm = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(cfg.hidden, dtype=cfg.dtype))
        self.moe_norm = nn.Parameter(torch.ones(cfg.hidden, dtype=cfg.dtype))
        self.attn = KDA(cfg) if kind == "K" else MLA(cfg)
        self.moe = MoE(cfg)

    def step(self, x, st):
        h = x + self.attn.step(_fast_rmsnorm(x, self.attn_norm), st)
        return h + self.moe.step(_fast_rmsnorm(h, self.moe_norm))


class Model(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        self.blocks = nn.ModuleList(Block(cfg, k) for k in cfg.pattern)

    def step(self, hidden, state):
        for i, blk in enumerate(self.blocks):
            hidden = blk.step(hidden, state[i])
        return hidden, state

user
I need you to make batch-1 autoregressive decode of a Kimi-Linear hybrid block as fast as possible on the RTX PRO 6000 (SM120 Blackwell, GDDR7, 1.8 TB/s). The model is W4A16: the big projection weights are stored as 4-bit integers, the activations and accumulation are bf16. reference.py is the correctness oracle and baseline.py is an already-optimized pure-PyTorch version; your job is to go beyond baseline.py. Your answer goes in solution.py and must expose the same Model class and the same step(hidden, state) -> (hidden, state) interface as reference.py, with identical buffer/parameter names so it loads the reference weights. Make whatever mess you want in this directory otherwise. The unit is one repeating motif of Kimi-Linear-48B-A3B: four layers in the pattern [KDA, KDA, KDA, MLA], each followed by a 64-expert MoE FFN (top-8 routed + 1 shared, SiLU, intermediate 1024), with RMSNorm and residuals. Hidden size is 2304. The KDA layers are gated-delta linear attention with 32 heads of dim 128, a short causal depthwise conv (kernel 4) on q/k/v, a per-channel log-decay gate, and a per-head write strength; they carry a fixed-size recurrent state S[32,128,128] plus the conv window across decode steps. The MLA layers are multi-head latent attention with 32 heads, a kv_lora_rank of 512, qk_nope 128, qk_rope 64, v_head 128, decoupled RoPE (theta 10000); they carry a growing compressed latent KV cache (the 512-d latent plus the 64-d rope key per past token). The weights are quantized W4A16, AWQ/GPTQ-style: per linear, the (in, out) weight is stored as int4 packed two-per-byte along `in` (w_q, uint8, shape (in//2, out)), with per-group asymmetric dequant params group-size 128 along `in` (scales and zeros, bf16, shape (in//128, out)). Dequant is w[k,n] = (unpack(w_q)[k,n] - zeros[k//128,n]) * scales[k//128,n]. The 64 MoE experts (and the shared expert) are stored the same way, one int4 weight set per expert. reference.py has the exact pack/unpack/dequant code, the layer math, the state layout, and how step consumes one token and updates both kinds of state. Read it. At batch 1 this decode is bandwidth-bound on the weight stream, and the int4 weights are a quarter of the bytes of bf16 - but only if you never materialize the dequantized bf16 weight. reference.py and baseline.py both unpack each weight to a full bf16 matrix and then matmul, which throws the bandwidth advantage away (int4 read plus bf16 write plus bf16 read). The job is to fuse the int4 unpack and per-group dequant directly into the GEMV so you stream the int4 weights once. You are decoding one new token against a context that is already `context_len` tokens long (the states and caches are pre-filled). Correctness is the next-token hidden vector and the updated decode state matching reference.py by cosine similarity (>= 0.98), checked from an identical fed state across several seeds and context lengths. You are scored on decode latency relative to baseline.py, geomean over context lengths 2048, 8192, and 16384. This needs to be real. Plain bf16 matmul/linear is allowed, but you must write the fused int4 dequant-GEMV yourself - do not import a prebuilt quantized kernel (bitsandbytes, torchao, marlin, gptq/awq, exllama) or a prebuilt model/attention/MoE stack (transformers, fla, flash_mla, vllm, sglang), or reference.py / baseline.py. If you need background, look up W4A16 / AWQ / GPTQ dequant-GEMV kernels, the Kimi-Linear architecture, KDA / gated DeltaNet, multi-head latent attention, and Blackwell/Triton decode kernels yourself. Your flywheel is implement, profile (ncu, nsys, torch.profiler - whatever helps) and time it with benchmark.py, verify correctness by running `python check.py` and reading the output, then iterate. Do not substitute your own one-off checks for check.py - it tests every layer type and the state update across seeds, your spot-check almost certainly will not. If `python check.py` has not printed PASS, you are not done. Take as long as you need to actually push the latency down. """PyTorch reference for a Kimi-Linear W4A16 hybrid decode unit (batch=1).

Correctness oracle, NOT the fast baseline (baseline.py) or the SOTA ceiling.
One repeating motif of Kimi-Linear-48B-A3B -- 3 KDA (gated-delta linear attn)
layers + 1 MLA (multi-head latent attention) layer, each + a 64-expert MoE FFN
-- decoded one token at a time, with the big projection weights stored as
**W4A16** (int4 weights, group-128 asymmetric, bf16 accumulation; the AWQ/GPTQ
format that open-source inference actually ships).

Why W4A16 and not fp8: at batch-1 decode the bottleneck is *weight memory
traffic*. int4 weights are 0.25x the bytes of bf16 (4x less traffic), and a
fused dequant-GEMV realizes that win in the memory-bound regime where decode
lives -- unlike fp8 tensor-core matmul, which has fixed overhead and loses at
M=1. int4/bf16-acc also needs no special tensor-core format, so it runs on any
bf16-capable GPU (Ampere, Hopper, Blackwell).

The two decode states are unchanged: KDA carries a fixed-size recurrent state
S[H,Dk,Dv] + short-conv window; MLA carries a growing compressed latent KV
cache. `step(hidden, state) -> (hidden, state)` consumes one token.

This reference dequantizes naively (unpack -> bf16 matrix -> matmul). The whole
problem is to FUSE the int4 unpack+dequant into the GEMV and never materialize
the bf16 weight. Pack format is identical to KernelBench-Hard proble

"""Optimized-PyTorch W4A16 baseline for the Kimi-Linear decode unit.

The floor the solution must beat -- NOT the oracle (reference.py). Same int4
weights, same math, written the competent pure-PyTorch way: bf16 accumulation
and batched MoE expert dequant instead of the reference's fp32 per-expert loop.

It still *materializes* each dequantized bf16 weight before the matmul (int4
read + bf16 write + bf16 read = ~9x the traffic of a fused path). That is the
whole point left on the table: stock PyTorch cannot fuse the int4 unpack into
the GEMV, so beating this baseline requires a custom fused dequant-GEMV kernel.
`score = baseline_latency / solution_latency`.
"""

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import torch.nn.functional as F

init_token = R.init_token

def _wbf(ql) -> torch.Tensor:
    return ql.weight_bf()  # [in, out] bf16


class KDA(R.KDA):
    def step(self, x, st):
        H, Dk = self.cfg.kda_heads, self.cfg.kda_head_dim
        q = x @ _wbf(self.q_proj)
        k = x @ _wbf(self.k_proj)
        v = x @ _wbf(self.v_proj)
        q, st["cq"] = self._short_conv(q, st["cq"], 0)
        k, st["ck"] = self._short_conv(k, st["ck"], 1)
        v, st["cv"] = self

"""Correctness runner for the Kimi-Linear hybrid decode unit.

Per-step correctness, not a chained trajectory: for each seed and a couple of
context lengths, the reference and the solution are given an IDENTICAL fed
state and one new token, each runs ONE decode step, and we compare the

precisions diverge, which is not a kernel-correctness signal.

    return F.cosine_similarity(a.float().flatten(), b.float().flatten(), dim=0).item()

"""Latency benchmark for the Kimi-Linear hybrid decode unit.

Score = baseline_latency / solution_latency (speedup over the optimized-PyTorch
baseline.py), geomean over the context-length sweep. The solution is timed
first; a final next-token check against the reference makes a fast-but-wrong
solution score zero. Absolute tok/s at the longest context is the shippable
"single-GPU decode" number.

Reported in the peak_fraction field as a speedup multiple (>1 means faster than
the baseline), not a [0,1] roofline fraction.
"""
from __future__ import annotations

import sys
import time
from math import exp, log
from pathlib import Path

import torch
import yaml


def _run(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed, ref):
    h = ref.init_token(cfg, seed)
    st = ref.init_state(cfg, ctx, seed)
    with torch.no_grad():
        for _ in range(steps):
            h, st = model.step(h, st)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    return h


def _time(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed, ref):
    _run(model, cfg, ctx, min(3, steps), seed, ref)   # warmup
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    best = float("inf")
    for _ in range(int(yaml.safe_load(Path("problem.yaml").read_text()).get("num_perf_trials", 3))):
        t0 = time.perf_counter()
        h = _run(model, cfg, ctx, steps, seed, ref)
        best = min(best, time.perf_counter() - t0)
    return best, h

    import baseline

class MoE(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, cfg: Config):
        super().__init__()
        self.cfg = cfg
        d, m, E = cfg.hidden, cfg.moe_inter, cfg.n_experts
        self.router = nn.Linear(d, E, bias=False, dtype=cfg.dtype)   # tiny, bf16
        self.gate = QuantExperts(E, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.up = QuantExperts(E, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.down = QuantExperts(E, m, d, cfg.group)
        self.s_gate = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.s_up = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, d, m, cfg.group)
        self.s_down = QuantExperts(cfg.n_shared, m, d, cfg.group)

    def _ffn(self, x, experts_g, experts_u, experts_d, e):
        h = F.silu(x.float() @ experts_g.weight_bf(e).float()) * (x.float() @ experts_u.weight_bf(e).float())
        return h @ experts_d.weight_bf(e).float()

    def step(self, x):
        cfg = self.cfg
        probs = torch.softmax(self.router(x).float(), dim=-1)
        w, idx = torch.topk(probs, cfg.n_active)
        w = w / (w.sum() + 1e-9) * cfg.routed_scaling
        out = x.new_zeros(cfg.hidden, dtype=torch.float32)
        for j in range(cfg.n_active):
            out = out + w[j] * self._ffn(x, self.gate, self.up, self.down, int(idx[j]))
        for s in range(cfg.n_shared):
            out = out + self._ffn(x, self.s_gate, self.s_up, self.s_down, s)
        return out.to(torch.bfloat16)

"""Decode shapes for the Kimi-Linear hybrid unit.

Score is latency speedup over baseline.py, so the sweep is over decode context
length. The long-context shape is where the architecture's design (fixed-size
KDA state + compressed MLA latent cache) pays off and where the absorb-vs-
materialize fork in MLA decides the whole thing -- that is the shippable "wow".

`n_experts` is 64 for v0 (real Kimi-Linear-48B-A3B is 256); bump it once the
problem is calibrated. `steps` is how many tokens to decode autoregressively
when timing (fewer at long context to bound wall time).
"""

+++ b//home/shadeform/mega/outputs/runs/20260618_162338_codex_gpt-5.5_03_kimi_linear_decode/repo/problems/03_kimi_linear_decode/solution.py

+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from dataclasses import dataclass, field
+
+import torch
+import torch.nn as nn
+import torch.nn.functional as F
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+EPS = 1.0e-6
+GROUP_SIZE = 128
+
+
+@dataclass(frozen=True)
+class Config:
+    hidden: int = 2304
+    kda_heads: int = 32
+    kda_head_dim: int = 128
+    short_conv: int = 4
+    mla_heads: int = 32
+    kv_lora: int = 512
+    qk_nope: int = 128
+    qk_rope: int = 64
+    v_head: int = 128
+    rope_theta: float = 10000.0
+    n_experts: int = 64
+    n_active: int = 8
+    n_shared: int = 1
+    moe_inter: int = 1024
+    routed_scaling: float = 2.446
+    group: int = 128
+    pattern: tuple = ("K", "K", "K", "M")
+    dtype: torch.dtype = field(default=torch.bfloat16)
+
+
+def build_config(shape: dict) -> Config:
+    return Config(n_experts=int(shape.get("n_experts", 64)))
+
+
+def _rmsnorm(x: torch.Tensor, w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xf = x.float()
+    xf = xf * torch.rsqrt(xf.pow(2).mean(-1, keepdim=True) + EPS)
+    return (xf * w.float()).to(x.dtype)
+
+
+def _rope_cossin(pos: int, dim: int, theta: float, device):
+    inv = 1.0 / (theta ** (torch.arange(0, dim, 2, device=device, dtype=torch.float32) / dim))
+    ang = pos * inv
+    return torch.cos(ang), torch.sin(ang)
+
+
+def _apply_rope(x: torch.Tensor, cos: torch.Tensor, sin: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xf = x.float()
+    even, odd = xf[..., 0::2], xf[..., 1::2]
+    out = torch.empty_like(xf)
+    out[..., 0::2] = even * cos - odd * sin
+    out[..., 1::2] = odd * cos + even * sin
+    return out.to(x.dtype)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _gemv_kernel(x, wq, scales, zeros, y, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr,
+                 BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
+    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
+        p = p0 + offs_p
+        byte = tl.load(wq + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
+        group = p // 64
+        s = tl.load(scales + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        z = tl.load(zeros + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        x0 = tl.load(x + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
+        x1 = tl.load(x + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
+        lo = (byte & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        hi = ((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        acc += tl.sum(((lo - z) * x0 + (hi - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
+    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=offs_n < N)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _gemv4_kernel(x, wq0, sc0, ze0, y0, wq1, sc1, ze1, y1, wq2, sc2, ze2, y2,
+                  wq3, sc3, ze3, y3, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr,
+                  BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
+    acc0 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    acc1 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    acc2 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    acc3 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
+        p = p0 + offs_p
+        group = p // 64
+        x0 = tl.load(x + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
+        x1 = tl.load(x + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
+
+        byte = tl.load(wq0 + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
+        s = tl.load(sc0 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        z = tl.load(ze0 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc0 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
+
+        byte = tl.load(wq1 + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
+        s = tl.load(sc1 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        z = tl.load(ze1 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc1 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
+
+        byte = tl.load(wq2 + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
+        s = tl.load(sc2 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        z = tl.load(ze2 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc2 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
+
+        byte = tl.load(wq3 + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
+        s = tl.load(sc3 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        z = tl.load(ze3 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc3 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
+
+    tl.store(y0 + offs_n, acc0, mask=offs_n < N)
+    tl.store(y1 + offs_n, acc1, mask=offs_n < N)
+    tl.store(y2 + offs_n, acc2, mask=offs_n < N)
+    tl.store(y3 + offs_n, acc3, mask=offs_n < N)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _expert_gemv2_kernel(x, idx, wq0, sc0, ze0, y0, wq1, sc1, ze1, y1,
+                         K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
+                         BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
+    e = tl.load(idx + pid_e)
+    offs_n = pid_

... (15190 more chars)

+from __future__ import annotations
+
+from dataclasses import dataclass, field
+
+import torch
+import torch.nn as nn
+import torch.nn.functional as F
+import triton
+import triton.language as tl
+
+EPS = 1.0e-6
+GROUP_SIZE = 128
+
+
+@dataclass(frozen=True)
+class Config:
+    hidden: int = 2304
+    kda_heads: int = 32
+    kda_head_dim: int = 128
+    short_conv: int = 4
+    mla_heads: int = 32
+    kv_lora: int = 512
+    qk_nope: int = 128
+    qk_rope: int = 64
+    v_head: int = 128
+    rope_theta: float = 10000.0
+    n_experts: int = 64
+    n_active: int = 8
+    n_shared: int = 1
+    moe_inter: int = 1024
+    routed_scaling: float = 2.446
+    group: int = 128
+    pattern: tuple = ("K", "K", "K", "M")
+    dtype: torch.dtype = field(default=torch.bfloat16)
+
+
+def build_config(shape: dict) -> Config:
+    return Config(n_experts=int(shape.get("n_experts", 64)))
+
+
+def _rmsnorm(x: torch.Tensor, w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xf = x.float()
+    xf = xf * torch.rsqrt(xf.pow(2).mean(-1, keepdim=True) + EPS)
+    return (xf * w.float()).to(x.dtype)
+
+
+def _rope_cossin(pos: int, dim: int, theta: float, device):
+    inv = 1.0 / (theta ** (torch.arange(0, dim, 2, device=device, dtype=torch.float32) / dim))
+    ang = pos * inv
+    return torch.cos(ang), torch.sin(ang)
+
+
+def _apply_rope(x: torch.Tensor, cos: torch.Tensor, sin: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    xf = x.float()
+    even, odd = xf[..., 0::2], xf[..., 1::2]
+    out = torch.empty_like(xf)
+    out[..., 0::2] = even * cos - odd * sin
+    out[..., 1::2] = odd * cos + even * sin
+    return out.to(x.dtype)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _gemv_kernel(x, wq, scales, zeros, y, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr,
+                 BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
+    acc = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
+        p = p0 + offs_p
+        byte = tl.load(wq + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
+        group = p // 64
+        s = tl.load(scales + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        z = tl.load(zeros + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        x0 = tl.load(x + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
+        x1 = tl.load(x + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
+        lo = (byte & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        hi = ((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32)
+        acc += tl.sum(((lo - z) * x0 + (hi - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
+    tl.store(y + offs_n, acc, mask=offs_n < N)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _gemv4_kernel(x, wq0, sc0, ze0, y0, wq1, sc1, ze1, y1, wq2, sc2, ze2, y2,
+                  wq3, sc3, ze3, y3, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr,
+                  BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(0)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
+    acc0 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    acc1 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    acc2 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    acc3 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
+        p = p0 + offs_p
+        group = p // 64
+        x0 = tl.load(x + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
+        x1 = tl.load(x + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
+
+        byte = tl.load(wq0 + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
+        s = tl.load(sc0 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        z = tl.load(ze0 + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc0 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) *

+@triton.jit
+def _expert_gemv2_kernel(x, idx, wq0, sc0, ze0, y0, wq1, sc1, ze1, y1,
+    tl.store(y0 + out, acc0, mask=offs_n < N)
+    tl.store(y1 + out, acc1, mask=offs_n < N)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _expert_hidden_kernel(x, idx, wq0, sc0, ze0, wq1, sc1, ze1, y,
+                          K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr, NG: tl.constexpr,
+                          BLOCK_N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_P: tl.constexpr):
+    pid_e = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_n = tl.program_id(1)
+    e = tl.load(idx + pid_e)
+    offs_n = pid_n * BLOCK_N + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_N)
+    offs_p = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_P)
+    acc0 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    acc1 = tl.zeros((BLOCK_N,), tl.float32)
+    w_base = e * ((K // 2) * N)
+    q_base = e * (NG * N)
+    for p0 in range(0, K // 2, BLOCK_P):
+        p = p0 + offs_p
+        group = p // 64
+        x0 = tl.load(x + 2 * p).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
+        x1 = tl.load(x + 2 * p + 1).to(tl.float32)[:, None]
+
+        byte = tl.load(wq0 + w_base + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
+        s = tl.load(sc0 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        z = tl.load(ze0 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc0 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
+
+        byte = tl.load(wq1 + w_base + p[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0)
+        s = tl.load(sc1 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        z = tl.load(ze1 + q_base + group[:, None] * N + offs_n[None, :], mask=offs_n[None, :] < N, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+        acc1 += tl.sum((((byte & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x0 + (((byte >> 4) & 15).to(tl.float32) - z) * x1) * s, axis=0)
+    h = (acc0 * tl.sigmoid(acc0)) * acc1
+    tl.store(y + pid_e * N + offs_n, h, mask=offs_n < N)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _expert_down_sum_kernel(x, route_w, idx, wq, scales, zeros, y,
+    def _hidden(self, x, idx, gate, up):
+        cfg = self.cfg
+        y = torch.empty((idx.numel(), cfg.moe_inter), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+        _expert_hidden_kernel[(idx.numel(), triton.cdiv(cfg.moe_inter, 32))](
+            x, idx, gate.w_q, gate.scales, gate.zeros, up.w_q, up.scales, up.zeros, y,
+            gate.in_f, gate.out_f, gate.in_f // gate.group, BLOCK_N=32, BLOCK_P=64,
+            num_warps=4,
+        )
+        return y
+        h = self._hidden(x, idx, self.gate, self.up)
+        out = self._down_sum(h, w, idx, self.down)
+        sh = self._hidden(x, self._shared_idx, self.s_gate, self.s_up)
+        return self._down_sum(sh, self._shared_w, self._shared_idx, self.s_down, out=out, add=True)

The remaining PyTorch overhead is mostly KDA plumbing: three depthwise short convolutions per KDA layer implemented with cat, casts, reductions, and SiLU. I’m replacing those with one Triton kernel per KDA layer that also updates the conv windows in place.

+@triton.jit
+def _short_conv3_kernel(q, k, v, cq, ck, cv, conv_w, C: tl.constexpr, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
+    offs = tl.program_id(0) * BLOCK + tl.arange(0, BLOCK)
+    mask = offs < C
+
+    qv = tl.load(q + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    p0 = tl.load(cq + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    p1 = tl.load(cq + C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    p2 = tl.load(cq + 2 * C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w0 = tl.load(conv_w + offs * 4, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w1 = tl.load(conv_w + offs * 4 + 1, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w2 = tl.load(conv_w + offs * 4 + 2, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w3 = tl.load(conv_w + offs * 4 + 3, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    out = p0 * w0 + p1 * w1 + p2 * w2 + qv * w3
+    tl.store(q + offs, out * tl.sigmoid(out), mask=mask)
+    tl.store(cq + offs, p1, mask=mask)
+    tl.store(cq + C + offs, p2, mask=mask)
+    tl.store(cq + 2 * C + offs, qv, mask=mask)
+
+    kv = tl.load(k + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    p0 = tl.load(ck + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    p1 = tl.load(ck + C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    p2 = tl.load(ck + 2 * C + offs, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    base = C * 4
+    w0 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w1 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4 + 1, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w2 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4 + 2, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    w3 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4 + 3, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    out = p0 * w0 + p1 * w1 + p2 * w2 + kv * w3
+    tl.store(k + offs, out * tl.sigmoid(out), mask=mask)
+    tl.store(ck + offs, p1, mask=mask)
+    tl.store(ck + C + offs, p2, mask=mask)

+    w3 = tl.load(conv_w + base + offs * 4 + 3, mask=mask, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)

 @triton.jit
+def _kda_recur_kernel(q, k, v, gp, beta, S, o, D: tl.constexpr,
+                      SCALE: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_V: tl.constexpr):
+    h = tl.program_id(0)
+    pid_v = tl.program_id(1)
+    offs_d = tl.arange(0, 128)
+    offs_v = pid_v * BLOCK_V + tl.arange(0, BLOCK_V)
+    base = h * D
+    s_base = h * D * D
+    s_offs = s_base + offs_d[:, None] * D + offs_v[None, :]
+
+    qv = tl.load(q + base + offs_d).to(tl.float32) * SCALE
+    kv = tl.load(k + base + offs_d).to(tl.float32)
+    gv = tl.load(gp + base + offs_d).to(tl.float32)
+    decay = tl.sigmoid(-gv)
+    vv = tl.load(v + base + offs_v, mask=offs_v < D, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    b = tl.load(beta + h).to(tl.float32)
+
+    sold = tl.load(S + s_offs, mask=offs_v[None, :] < D, other=0.0).to(tl.float32)
+    sdec = sold * decay[:, None]
+    pred = tl.sum(sdec * kv[:, None], axis=0)
+    snew = sdec + (b * kv)[:, None] * (vv[None, :] - pred[None, :])
+    out = tl.sum(snew * qv[:, None], axis=0)
+
+    tl.store(S + s_offs, snew, mask=offs_v[None, :] < D)
+    tl.store(o + base + offs_v, out, mask=offs_v < D)
+
+

MoE still launches separate routed and shared expert kernels. I’m folding the shared expert into the routed kernels without concatenating weights: the new kernels branch internally for the ninth expert and use the shared weight tensors directly. This should reduce launch count and Python overhead.

@core._tensor_member_fn
@jit
@core._add_reduction_docstr("minimum index", tie_break_arg="tie_break_left")
def argmin(input, axis, tie_break_left=True, keep_dims=False):
    _, ret = min(input, axis, return_indices=True, return_indices_tie_break_left=tie_break_left, keep_dims=keep_dims)
    return ret


@jit
def _sum_combine(a, b):
    return a + b


# sum


@constexpr_function
def _pick_sum_dtype(in_dtype, dtype):
    if dtype is not None:
        return dtype

    # For integer bitwidths less than 32, pick int32 with the same sign to
    # avoid overflow.
    out_dtype = None
    if in_dtype.is_int_signed():
        out_dtype = core.int32 if in_dtype.int_bitwidth < 32 else None
    elif in_dtype.is_int_unsigned():
        out_dtype = core.uint32 if in_dtype.int_bitwidth < 32 else None
    return out_dtype


@core._tensor_member_fn
@jit
@core._add_reduction_docstr("sum", dtype_arg="dtype")
def sum(input, axis=None, keep_dims=False, dtype: core.constexpr = None):
    # Pick a default dtype for the reduction if one was not specified.
    out_dtype: core.constexpr = _pick_sum_dtype(input.dtype, dtype)

    if out_dtype is not None:
        input = input.to(out_dtype)
    return core.reduce(input, axis, _sum_combine, keep_dims=keep_dims)


@jit
def _xor_combine(a, b):
    return a ^ b

@jit
def _argmin_combine(value1, index1, value2, index2, tie_break_left):
    if tie_break_left:
        tie = value1 == value2 and index1 < index2
    else:
        tie = False
    lt = value1 < value2 or tie
    value_ret = core.where(lt, value1, value2)
    index_ret = core.where(lt, index1, index2)
    return value_ret, index_ret

+@triton.jit
+def _rmsnorm_kernel(x, w, y, N: tl.constexpr, BLOCK: tl.constexpr):
+    tl.store(y + offs, xv * r * wv, mask=mask)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _router_kernel(x, weight, idx_out, w_out, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr,
+                   SCALE: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    offs_n = tl.arange(0, 64)
+    offs_k = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+    acc = tl.zeros((64,), tl.float32)
+    for k0 in range(0, K, BLOCK_K):
+        kk = k0 + offs_k
+        xv = tl.load(x + kk).to(tl.float32)[None, :]
+        wv = tl.load(weight + offs_n[:, None] * K + kk[None, :]).to(tl.float32)
+        acc += tl.sum(wv * xv, axis=1)
+
+    vals = acc
+    m0, i0 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
+    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i0, -float("inf"), vals)
+    m1, i1 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
+    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i1, -float("inf"), vals)
+    m2, i2 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
+    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i2, -float("inf"), vals)
+    m3, i3 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
+    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i3, -float("inf"), vals)
+    m4, i4 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
+    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i4, -float("inf"), vals)
+    m5, i5 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
+    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i5, -float("inf"), vals)
+    m6, i6 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
+    vals = tl.where(offs_n == i6, -float("inf"), vals)
+    m7, i7 = tl.max(vals, axis=0, return_indices=True)
+
+    e0 = 1.0
+    e1 = tl.exp(m1 - m0)
+    e2 = tl.exp(m2 - m0)
+    e3 = tl.exp(m3 - m0)
+    e4 = tl.exp(m4 - m0)
+    e5 = tl.exp(m5 - m0)
+    e6 = tl.exp(m6 - m0)
+    e7 = tl.exp(m7 - m0)
+    den = e0 + e1 + e2 + e3 + e4 + e5 + e6 + e7 + 1.0e-9
+    s = SCALE / den
+    tl.store(idx_out + 0, i0)
+    tl.store(idx_out + 1, i1)
+    tl.store(idx_out + 2, i2)
+    tl.store(idx_out + 3, i3)
+    tl.store(idx_out + 4, i4)
+    tl.store(idx_out + 5, i5)
+    tl.store(idx_out + 6, i6)
+    tl.store(idx_out + 7, i7)
+    tl.store(w_out + 0, e0 * s)
+    tl.store(w_out + 1, e1 * s)
+    tl.store(w_out + 2, e2 * s)
+    tl.store(w_out + 3, e3 * s)
+    tl.store(w_out + 4, e4 * s)
+    tl.store(w_out + 5, e5 * s)
+    tl.store(w_out + 6, e6 * s)
+    tl.store(w_out + 7, e7 * s)
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _gemv_kernel(x, wq, scales, zeros, y, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr,
+def _fast_rmsnorm(x: torch.Tensor, w: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+    y = torch.empty_like(x)
+    _rmsnorm_kernel[(1,)](x, w, y, x.numel(), BLOCK=4096, num_warps=8)
+    return y
+
+
+def _route(x: torch.Tensor, router: nn.Linear, scaling: float):
+    idx = torch.empty((8,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.long)
+    w = torch.empty((8,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16)
+    _router_kernel[(1,)](x, router.weight, idx, w, x.numel(), router.out_features, scaling,
+                         BLOCK_K=256, num_warps=8)
+    return w, idx

+@triton.jit
+def _router_kernel(x, weight, idx_out, w_out, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr,
+    tl.store(w_out + 7, e7 * s)

+
+@triton.jit
+def _beta_kernel(x, weight, y, K: tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K: tl.constexpr):
+    offs_n = tl.arange(0, 32)
+    offs_k = tl.arange(0, BLOCK_K)
+    acc = tl.zeros((32,), tl.float32)
+    for k0 in range(0, K, BLOCK_K):
+        kk = k0 + offs_k
+        xv = tl.load(x + kk).to(tl.float32)[None, :]
+        wv = tl.load(weight + offs_n[:, None] * K + kk[None, :]).to(tl.float32)
+        acc += tl.sum(wv * xv, axis=1)
+    tl.store(y + offs_n, tl.sigmoid(acc))
+
+
+@triton.jit
+def _gemv_kernel(x, wq, scales, zeros, y, K: tl.constexpr, N: tl.constexpr,
+def _route(x: torch.Tensor, router: nn.Linear, scaling: float):
+    return w, idx
+
+
+def _beta(x: torch.Tensor, proj: nn.Linear) -> torch.Tensor:
+    y = torch.empty((32,), device=x.device, dtype=torch.float32)
+    _beta_kernel[(1,)](x, proj.weight, y, x.numel(), BLOCK_K=256, num_warps=4)
+    return y

import torch,time,triton
import reference as ref, solution
cfg=ref.build_config({'n_experts':64}); dev='cuda:0'
rm=ref.Model(cfg).to(dev).eval(); m=solution.Model(cfg).to(dev).eval(); m.load_state_dict(rm.state_dict(), strict=True)
x=ref.init_token(cfg,101); beta=m.blocks[0].attn.beta_proj; moe=m.blocks[0].moe

def bench_beta(BK,warps,it=100):
 y=torch.empty((32,),device=dev,dtype=torch.float32)
 try:
  solution._beta_kernel[(1,)](x,beta.weight,y,2304,BLOCK_K=BK,num_warps=warps)
  torch.cuda.synchronize(); t0=time.perf_counter()
  for _ in range(it): solution._beta_kernel[(1,)](x,beta.weight,y,2304,BLOCK_K=BK,num_warps=warps)
  torch.cuda.synchronize(); return (time.perf_counter()-t0)*1e6/it
 except Exception as e: return 'ERR '+str(e).split('\n')[0]
for BK in [32,64,128,256,512]:
 for w in [1,2,4,8]: print('beta',BK,w,bench_beta(BK,w,50), flush=True)

def bench_router(BK,warps,it=100):
 idx=torch.empty((8,),device=dev,dtype=torch.long); wt=torch.empty((8,),device=dev,dtype=torch.bfloat16)
 try:
  solution._router_kernel[(1,)](x,moe.router.weight,idx,wt,2304,64,2.446,BLOCK_K=BK,num_warps=warps)
  torch.cuda.synchronize(); t0=time.perf_counter()
  for _ in range(it): solution._router_kernel[(1,)](x,moe.router.weight,idx,wt,2304,64,2.446,BLOCK_K=BK,num_warps=warps)
  torch.cuda.synchronize(); return (time.perf_counter()-t0)*1e6/it
 except Exception as e: return 'ERR '+str(e).split('\n')[0]
for BK in [32,64,128,256,512]:
 for w in [1,2,4,8]: print('router',BK,w,bench_router(BK,w,50), flush=True)

import torch,time,triton,triton.language as tl
import reference as ref, solution

@triton.jit
def router_dot(x, weight, idx_out, w_out, K:tl.constexpr, SCALE:tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K:tl.constexpr):
    offs_n=tl.arange(0,64)
    offs_k=tl.arange(0,BLOCK_K)
    acc=tl.zeros((1,64),tl.float32)
    for k0 in range(0,K,BLOCK_K):
        kk=k0+offs_k
        xv=tl.load(x+kk)[None,:]
        wv=tl.load(weight+offs_n[None,:]*K+kk[:,None])
        acc += tl.dot(xv,wv,out_dtype=tl.float32)
    vals=tl.reshape(acc,(64,))
    m0,i0=tl.max(vals,axis=0,return_indices=True); vals=tl.where(offs_n==i0,-float('inf'),vals)
    m1,i1=tl.max(vals,axis=0,return_indices=True); vals=tl.where(offs_n==i1,-float('inf'),vals)
    m2,i2=tl.max(vals,axis=0,return_indices=True); vals=tl.where(offs_n==i2,-float('inf'),vals)
    m3,i3=tl.max(vals,axis=0,return_indices=True); vals=tl.where(offs_n==i3,-float('inf'),vals)
    m4,i4=tl.max(vals,axis=0,return_indices=True); vals=tl.where(offs_n==i4,-float('inf'),vals)
    m5,i5=tl.max(vals,axis=0,return_indices=True); vals=tl.where(offs_n==i5,-float('inf'),vals)
    m6,i6=tl.max(vals,axis=0,return_indices=True); vals=tl.where(offs_n==i6,-float('inf'),vals)
    m7,i7=tl.max(vals,axis=0,return_indices=True)
    e0=1.0; e1=tl.exp(m1-m0); e2=tl.exp(m2-m0); e3=tl.exp(m3-m0); e4=tl.exp(m4-m0); e5=tl.exp(m5-m0); e6=tl.exp(m6-m0); e7=tl.exp(m7-m0)
    s=SCALE/(e0+e1+e2+e3+e4+e5+e6+e7+1e-9)
    tl.store(idx_out+0,i0); tl.store(idx_out+1,i1); tl.store(idx_out+2,i2); tl.store(idx_out+3,i3); tl.store(idx_out+4,i4); tl.store(idx_out+5,i5); tl.store(idx_out+6,i6); tl.store(idx_out+7,i7)
    tl.store(w_out+0,e0*s); tl.store(w_out+1,e1*s); tl.store(w_out+2,e2*s); tl.store(w_out+3,e3*s); tl.store(w_out+4,e4*s); tl.store(w_out+5,e5*s); tl.store(w_out+6,e6*s); tl.store(w_out+7,e7*s)

@triton.jit
def beta_dot(x, weight, y, K:tl.constexpr, BLOCK_K:tl.constexpr):
    offs_n=tl.arange(0,32); offs_k=tl.arange(0,BLOCK_K)
    acc=tl.zeros((1,32),tl.float32)
    for k0 in range(0,K,BLOCK_K):
        kk=k0+offs_k
        xv=tl.load(x+kk)[None,:]
        wv=tl.load(weight+offs_n[None,:]*K+kk[:,None])
        acc += tl.dot(xv,wv,out_dtype=tl.float32)
    vals=tl.reshape(acc,(32,))
    tl.store(y+offs_n,tl.sigmoid(vals))
